    eol ::= <%!idChar> {10} [registerNewline] // token

    ws* ::= [ws*] <%!idChar> ws // $
    ws* ::= [ws*] <%!idChar> ws // token
    ws* ::= [ws*] <%!idChar> ws // ws
        !idChar => move: 213
        <test> => move: 123

    ws* ::= [ws*] <%!idChar> ws // $
